    3076             : /* test_thread_state spawns a thread of its own, and that thread releases
    3077             :  * `thread_done` when it's finished.  The driver code has to know when the
    3078             :  * thread finishes, because the thread uses a PyObject (the callable) that
    3079             :  * may go away when the driver finishes.  The former lack of this explicit
    3080             :  * synchronization caused rare segfaults, so rare that they were seen only
    3081             :  * on a Mac buildbot (although they were possible on any box).
    3082             :  */
